The hotel belongs to the hotel series of Puyuan Ancient Town. After recording your face, you can enter and exit the ancient town unlimited times on the day of check-in and check-out. I upgraded to a room with a balcony for free. The hotel's own courtyard is quite elegant. The fruit for check-in is cherry tomatoes, which feels a bit simple. In the evening, I gave them tangerine peel and red beans. The taste is average, but it is more considerate to put them in a thermos bottle.

Facilities:
The bug point is that there is no main switch, and it is quite tiring to turn off the lights one by one.

The ancient town is very large and has few people. Although there is not much development and few supporting restaurants, it is quiet and beautiful and very photogenic.
